  logger -p local1.debug "This is normal log -> debug"
  echo 'local1.*                                                /var/log/mylog.debug' >> /etc/rsyslog.conf

  logger -p local2.err "This is error -> error"
  echo 'local2.*                                                                                          /var/log/mylog.error' >> /etc/rsyslog.conf

  logger -p local3.crit "This is critical error -> crit"
  echo 'local3.*                                                                                          /var/log/mylog.crit' >> /etc/rsyslog.conf

  sudo systemctl restart rsyslog

  #sudo touch /etc/logrotate.d/mylogdebug.conf
  #sudo touch /etc/logrotate.d/mylogerror.conf
  #sudo touch /etc/logrotate.d/mylogcrit.conf

      dateext
      daily
      rotate 5
      compress
  }' > /etc/logrotate.d/mylogdebug.conf
  sudo logrotate -f /etc/logrotate.d/mylogdebug.conf

  {
          dateext
          daily
          rotate 5
      delaycompress
  }' > /etc/logrotate.d/mylogerror.conf
  sudo logrotate -f /etc/logrotate.d/mylogerror.conf

  {
          dateext
          weekly
          rotate 5
  }' > /etc/logrotate.d/mylogcrit.conf

  Decision:
  #!/bin/bash
  while [[ True ]]
  do
      echo "enter your name:"
      read name
      if [[ $name == "" ]]
      then
          echo "bye"
          break
      fi
      echo "enter your age:"
      read age
      if [[ $age == 0 ]]
      then    
          echo "bye"
          break
      elif [[ $age -le 16 ]]
      then
          echo "$name, your group is child"
      elif [[ $age -ge 17 && $age -le 25 ]]
      then
          echo "$name, your group is youth"
      else
          echo "$name, your group is adult"
      fi
  done

  Decision:
  #!/bin/bash
  PROGNAME=$(basename $0)
  usage () {
      cat <<- EOF
      Usage: $PROGNAME PRINCIPAL INTEREST MONTHS
      Where:
      PRINCIPAL is the amount of the loan.
      INTEREST is the APR as a number (7% = 0.07).
      MONTHS is the length of the loan's term.
      EOF
  }
  if (($# != 3)); then
      usage
      exit 1
  fi
  principal=$1
  interest=$2
  months=$3
  bc <<- EOF
      scale = 10
      i = $interest / 12
      p = $principal
      n = $months
      a = p * ((i * ((1 + i) ^ n)) / (((1 + i) ^ n) - 1))
      print a, "\n"
      EOF
  Task:

  aboutuser() {
      read -p "About user: " line
      cat /etc/passwd | grep -w $line
  }
  adduser(){
      read -p "Add user: " name
          #cut -d':' -f1 /etc/passwd | grep -w $name

          #cut -d':' -f1 /etc/passwd | grep -w $name

  user() {
      select option in "About user" "Add user" "Delete user" "Exit"
      do
          case $option in
              "About user") aboutuser ;;
              "Add user") adduser ;;
              "Delete user") deleteuser ;;
              "Exit") break ;;
              *) echo Wrong option ;;
          esac
      done
  }

  read -p "Print username: " user

      then
          echo "+"
      else
          echo "-"
      fi
  else
      echo "command not found"
  fi

  for i in $(stat -c %y "$1"/* | cut -c 12-13); do

  echo -e "Hour\tFiles\tHour\tFiles"

      j=$((i + 12))
      printf "%02d\t%d\t%02d\t%d\n" $i ${hours[i]} $j ${hours[j]}
  done
  printf "\nTotal files = %d\n" $count

  #!/bin/bash
  # read-ifs: 
  FILE=/etc/passwd
  read -p "Enter a username > " user_name
  file_info=$(grep "^$user_name:" $FILE)
  if [ -n "$file_info" ]; then
      IFS=":" read user pw uid gid name home shell <<< "$file_info"
      echo "User = '$user'"
      echo "UID = '$uid'"
      echo "GID = '$gid'"

      echo "Home Dir. = '$home'"

  #!/bin/bash

  #!/bin/bash

  # –ø—É—Å—Ç–æ–π –≤–≤–æ–¥ (–Ω–µ–¥–æ–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏–º–æ)

      echo "'$REPLY' is a valid filename."
      if [[ -e $REPLY ]]; then
          echo "And file '$REPLY' exists."
      else
          echo "However, file '$REPLY' does not exist."
      fi
      # –≤–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–æ –≤–µ—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ —á–∏—Å–ª–æ?
      if [[ $REPLY =~ ^-?[[:digit:]]*\.[[:digit:]]+$ ]]; then
          echo "'$REPLY' is a floating point number."
      else
          echo "'$REPLY' is not a floating point number."
      fi
      # –≤–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–æ —Ü–µ–ª–æ–µ —á–∏—Å–ª–æ?
      if [[ $REPLY =~ ^-?[[:digit:]]+$ ]]; then
          echo "'$REPLY' is an integer."
      else
          echo "'$REPLY' is not an integer."
      fi
  else
      echo "The string '$REPLY' is not a valid filename."
  fi
  Task:
  –ü—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∞ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã —Å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π –æ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ
  Decision:
  #/bin/bash
  PROGNAME=$(basename $0)
  TITLE="System Information Report For $HOSTNAME"
  CURRENT_TIME=$(date +"%x %r %Z")
  TIME_STAMP="Generated $CURRENT_TIME, by $USER"
  report_uptime () {
      cat <<- _EOF_
          <H2>System Uptime</H2>
          <PRE>$(uptime)</PRE>
          _EOF_
      return
  }
  report_disk_space () {
      cat <<- _EOF_
          <H2>Disk Space Utilization</H2>
          <PRE>$(df -h)</PRE>
          _EOF_
      return
  }
  report_home_space () {
      local format="%8s%10s%10s\n"
      local i dir_list total_files total_dirs total_size user_name
      if [[ $(id -u) -eq 0 ]]; then
          dir_list=/home/*
          user_name="All Users"
      else
          dir_list=$HOME
          user_name=$USER
      fi
      echo "<H2>Home Space Utilization ($user_name)</H2>"
      for i in $dir_list; do   
          total_files=$(find $i -type f | wc -l)
          total_dirs=$(find $i -type d | wc -l)
          total_size=$(du -sh $i | cut -f 1)
          echo "<H3>$i</H3>"
          echo "<PRE>"
          printf "$format" "Dirs" "Files" "Size"
          printf "$format" "----" "-----" "----"
          printf "$format" $total_dirs $total_files $total_size
          echo "</PRE>"
      done
      return
  }
  usage () {
      echo "$PROGNAME: usage: $PROGNAME [-f file | -i]"
      return
  }
  write_html_page () {
      cat <<- _EOF_
      <HTML>
          <HEAD>
              <TITLE>$TITLE</TITLE>
          </HEAD>
          <BODY>
              <H1>$TITLE</H1>
              <P>$TIME_STAMP</P>
              $(report_uptime)
              $(report_disk_space)
              $(report_home_space)    
          </BODY>
      </HTML>
      _EOF_
      return
  }
  # –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∞ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–≤ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–Ω–æ–π —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏
  interactive=
  filename=
  while [[ -n $1 ]]; do
      case $1 in
      -f | --file)        shift
                  filename=$1
                  ;;
      -i | --interactive) interactive=1
                  ;;
      -h | --help)        usage
                  exit
                  ;;
      *)          usage >&2
                  exit 1
                  ;;
      esac
      shift
  done
  # –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º
  if [[ -n $interactive ]]; then
      while true; do
      read -p "Enter name of output file: " filename
          if [[ -e $filename ]]; then
              read -p "'$filename' exists. Overwrite? [y/n/q] > "
              case $REPLY in
                  Y|y)    break
                      ;;
                  Q|q)    echo "Program terminated."
                      exit
                      ;;
                  *)  continue
                      ;;
              esac
          fi
      done
  fi
  # –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã html
  if [[ -n $filename ]]; then
      if touch $filename && [[ -f $filename ]]; then
          write_html_page > $filename
      else
          echo "$PROGNAME: Cannot write file '$filename'" >&2
          exit 1
      fi
  else
      write_html_page
  fi
  Task:
  —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π –¥–ª—è –¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –≤–∏–¥–æ–≤ –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫
  Decision:

  if [[ "$int" =~ ^-?[0-9]+$ ]]; then
      if [ $int -eq 0 ]; then
          echo "$int is zero."
      else
          if [ $int -lt 0 ]; then
              echo "$int is negative."
          else
              echo "$int is positive."
          fi

          fi
      fi

      echo "Input value is not an integer." >&2
      exit 1
  fi

          # description: The telnet s serves telnet sessions; it uses \

  #!/bin/bash
  # –¢–∞–∫–∂–µ —É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è root —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ cron, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –æ–Ω –∫–∞–∂–¥—É—é –ø—è—Ç–Ω–∏—Ü—É –≤ 23:30 –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–ª —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–µ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏ /data –∏ —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–µ –∞—Ä—Ö–∏–≤–∞ /backup/archive.tar –≤ —Ñ–∞–π–ª /var/log/reports/—Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∞—è–¥–∞—Ç–∞.
  mkdir /var/log/reports
